<div class=\"col-12 col-4-tablet\">\n                            <div class=\"featured-description\">\n                                <p>Uma das animações mais nostálgicas dos anos 2000,&nbsp;As </div>\n            </div>\n                                    <div class=\"tab-content \" id=\"news-tab-9\">\n\n                <div class=\"posts\">\n                                    <div class=\"row gutter-6 space-bottom-lg\">\n                        <div class=\"col-12 col-8-tablet\">\n                           <div class=\"featured-box\">\n    <a class=\"title clear below\">\n\t\t<div class=\"block none-tablet mobile-title\" style=\"word-wrap: break-word;\">\n\t\t\tBTS: Grupo lidera nos views no YouTube\t\t</div>\n\t\n        <div class=\"title-line none block-tablet\">\n        BTS: Grupo lidera         </div>\n        <div class=\"title-line none block-tablet\">\n            nos views no YouTube         </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"postdate clear line-numbers-2  above\">\n        <time class=\"entry-date published\" datetime=\"2017-04-21T19:50:53+00:00\">21 abril, 2017</time><time class=\"updated\" datetime=\"2017-04-21T20:08:54+00:00\">21 abril, 2017</time>            </div>\n\n    \n    </a>\n</div>\n                        </div>\n                        <div class=\"col-12 col-4-tablet\">\n                            <div class=\"featured-description\">\n                                <p>De acordo com estatísticas&nbsp;calculadas pela Google e YouTube Insights, BTS é o atual grupo de
